              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=paranormal-uf">paranormal-uf</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=steamy">steamy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=romantic">romantic</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer348266356" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3674859150877307612">Love this! A solid 4.5 stars!<br/><br/>Both Wulf and Cassandra were great characters and I loved the originality of the way they came together. This led into a HUGELY exciting twist in the story, and I loved watching how the relationship all unfolded from there. And because all of this happened pretty early on in the book, we got some quality time with them as a couple… I love that!!!<br/><br/>This book had a bit of a different feel to it than the others I’ve read in the series. There was a lot more world-building </span>
  <span id="freeText3674859150877307612" style="display:none">Love this! A solid 4.5 stars!<br /><br />Both Wulf and Cassandra were great characters and I loved the originality of the way they came together. This led into a HUGELY exciting twist in the story, and I loved watching how the relationship all unfolded from there. And because all of this happened pretty early on in the book, we got some quality time with them as a couple… I love that!!!<br /><br />This book had a bit of a different feel to it than the others I’ve read in the series. There was a lot more world-building in this one, and we got to see into the Apollite / Daimon side of the story, which was interesting. And Wulf’s story was a little different from that of the other Dark Hunters - I’m enjoying how Kenyon manages to mix that up a bit to keep it interesting. <br /><br />There were a number of swoony moments, and lots of laughs. One of the highlights though was the coming together of all of the boys from the previous books. I had a very swoony moment picturing them all going out to fight together. And of course, Zarek is hilarious! I find him funnier in the two books where he is a side character then he was in his own book. <br /><br />I did wonder a little bit about <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ the uncertainty the characters experienced at the end of the book. If the love of my life was going to die a hideous, painful death I’d do anything I could to keep them alive… what’s a little biting and blood drinking amongst lovers? <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>. But that was quickly overcome (and how!) so I’m not overly upset by it. <br /><br />Quickly moving onto the next book in the series. Yay!<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="3674859150877307612" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1681018576" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17454231209619509079">After reading Zarek's book, I was almost sure nothing could be better than that book. And sadly, I was right. <br/><br/>I was excited, since I thought the 'can't remember Wulf after five minutes' plot was interesting, but instead I found myself waiting (and wanting) for this book to end. I find it hard to follow the mythology of the series sometimes, since it has too many characters, but I can overlook that (because it could only be me), but this book was particularly hard to follow and kind of pointless </span>
  <span id="freeText17454231209619509079" style="display:none">After reading Zarek's book, I was almost sure nothing could be better than that book. And sadly, I was right. <br /><br />I was excited, since I thought the 'can't remember Wulf after five minutes' plot was interesting, but instead I found myself waiting (and wanting) for this book to end. I find it hard to follow the mythology of the series sometimes, since it has too many characters, but I can overlook that (because it could only be me), but this book was particularly hard to follow and kind of pointless in my opinion. <br /><br />Actually, let me rephrase that: the point of this book was to make me feel sorry for the appollites. I guess. Either way, nobody dies (I'm not speaking about the secondary characters), nothings really happens other than Wulf and Cassandra talking, and talking, and taaaalking....<br /><br />So yeah, I didn't really 'learn' anything about the DH or Acheron and I didn't change what I think about the appollites. <br /><br />What I did enjoy was 1) when the characters from the previous books showed up, 2) when Chris told the other about how Wulf had being an overprotective parent, and the epilogue that showed it. <br /><br />One of my least favourites so far; but I will continue reading the series because I like how the author writes and portrays emotions; although I think I'll just skip to Acheron's book.<br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="17454231209619509079" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('rl3R+fPFX/6yix5hNvkOEVqSbyjmgNuuZe79EWbwFmOYNcmr6l0lR4hdor4tAtw+vjtC/fOmjlATE+NMYrnWpw==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('0sRlBHmuwVLgEkHWiq1Sk2JG45bcL1Vaenc4Pr7z+DTkrH1WYDa769rE/QmRVoC8hu/OQ8kJAKQMiiZjuro48A==')})
  }
//]]>

    n = load.length,
    i = 0,
    go = function () {
      for (i = 0; i < n; i += 1) {
        script = d.createElement('SCRIPT');
        script.type = 'text/javascript';
        script.async = true;
        script.src = load[i];
        first.parentNode.insertBefore(script, first);
      }
    }
  if (w.attachEvent) {
    w.attachEvent('onload', go);
  } else {
    w.addEventListener('load', go, false);
  }
}(window, document,
    ['//assets.pinterest.com/js/pinit.js',
     '//apis.google.com/js/plusone.js'
    ]
  ));

//]]>
</script>
